Abstract: Loan origination is the process by which a lender creates a new loan, from application and underwriting through approval and funding. This process serves a critical role in evaluating the eligibility and level of risk posed by an applicant. Recently, firms have begun using mortgage loan agents to augment human loan officers, despite a lack of any public benchmark. ### [80] [3D-DLP: Self-Supervised 3D Object-Centric Scene Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19451)
*Ellina Zhang,Madhaven Iyengar,Amir Zadeh,Chuan Li,Deepak Pathak,David Held,Tal Daniel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 3D-DLP 是一种新型自监督 3D 场景表示模型，它将场景分解为可操作的 3D 潜粒子，在提升机器人任务执行效率的同时，实现了对场景的高效与可解释性建模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 3D 场景表示方法往往缺乏物体中心化的结构信息，导致在处理复杂的机器人操作任务时，要么难以理解场景组成，要么因使用密集 3D 输入而导致计算开销过大。因此，作者旨在构建一种既具有 3D 空间感知能力，又具备物体级可解释性的表示学习框架。

Method: 提出了一种基于自监督学习的 3D-DLP 模型。该方法将场景的 RGB-D 或体素观测数据分解为一组 3D 潜粒子（Latent Particles）。每个粒子通过自监督重构目标进行训练，显式编码粒子的 3D 关键点位置、包围盒尺寸和外观特征，并生成可解释的粒子级分割图。

Result: 在仿真和真实世界数据集上的实验表明，3D-DLP 学习到的潜空间具有高度的可解释性和可控性，能够通过修改粒子参数生成新的场景布局。此外，在机器人操作任务中，使用 3D-DLP 的紧凑表示在性能上优于缺乏 3D 信息或依赖密集输入结构的基线模型。

Conclusion: 3D-DLP 成功将 3D 场景分解为可解释、可操作的潜空间粒子，为机器人操作任务提供了一种高效、结构化的场景表示方法，证明了物体中心化表示在 3D 视觉任务中的优越性。

Abstract: We introduce 3D-DLP, a self-supervised object-centric representation learning model that decomposes scene-level RGB-D or voxel observations into a set of 3D latent particles. Building on the Deep Latent Particles (DLP) framework, each particle encodes disentangled attributes, including 3D keypoint position, bounding box dimensions, and appearance features, and represents a distinct entity in the scene. The model learns interpretable per-particle segmentation maps through an end-to-end self-supervised reconstruction objective. We demonstrate on both simulated and real-world datasets that the learned latent space is interpretable and controllable: by manipulating particle positions and decoding, we can generate novel scene configurations. Furthermore, we show that leveraging these compact 3D latent particles for downstream robotic manipulation improves performance over baselines that either lack explicit 3D information or rely on memory-intensive dense 3D inputs without object-centric structure. Code and videos are available at https://eubooks3003.github.io/3d-dlp.

</details>


### [81] [Can In-Context Learning Support Intrinsic Curiosity?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19476)
*Eric Elmoznino,Sangnie Bhardwaj,Johannes von Oswald,Rajai Nasser,Blaise Agüera y Arcas,João Sacramento,Rif A. Saurous,Guillaume Lajoie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了利用大型语言模型或序列模型的上下文学习（ICL）能力替代传统梯度下降，来实现高效的“内在好奇心”驱动的数据探索。研究证明该方法在主动学习等非时间序列任务中表现出色，能有效且低成本地实现最优数据采集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于“学习进度”的内在好奇心方法依赖于昂贵的梯度下降内循环，难以在大规模场景下扩展。本文旨在探索利用序列模型涌现的上下文学习能力，消除这一计算瓶颈，实现更高效的自动化数据选择。

Method: 研究团队提出利用序列模型的上下文学习（ICL）能力作为无需参数更新的即时世界模型，通过预测误差和反事实上下文操作来构建探索奖励。研究从理论上分析了该方法在一般马尔可夫决策过程中的局限性，并证明了其在主动学习和贝叶斯实验设计等非时间序列子类问题中的有效性。

Result: 理论分析证明，在一般马尔可夫决策过程中无偏地估计学习进度是不可能的；但在主动学习和贝叶斯实验设计等广泛的非时间序列设置下，基于ICL的奖励能够有效界定并渐近收敛于真实的学习进度。实验结果证实，该框架能有效训练出具备最优探索能力的“好奇”数据采集策略。

Conclusion: 该研究通过理论证明和实验验证，确立了上下文学习（ICL）在非时间序列环境中替代传统梯度更新作为“内在好奇心”奖励机制的可行性，为实现大规模自动化数据选择提供了高效的新路径。

Abstract: Effective machine learning depends not only on how we model data, but also on what data we choose to collect. While large sequence models have revolutionized data modeling, the problem of automated data selection, or "intrinsic curiosity", remains a significant challenge. Classic approaches incentivize exploration by rewarding an agent based on its "learning progress", which measures how much a newly acquired observation improves a world model's predictive ability. However, evaluating these rewards traditionally requires expensive inner loops of gradient descent updates within each trajectory, rendering them computationally impractical at scale. In this work, we investigate whether the emergent in-context learning (ICL) capabilities of sequence models can eliminate this bottleneck by serving as immediate, update-free world models. Specifically, we evaluate whether an exploration policy can be trained to maximize learning progress, using solely the prediction errors and counterfactual context manipulations of an in-context learner. We first prove that in general Markov decision processes, this is in fact impossible in an unbiased way: the resulting intrinsic rewards either suffer from nuisance terms that bias their estimation of true learning progress, or they cannot be implemented using an in-context learner's prediction errors. Conversely, we prove a positive result for a broad subclass of non-temporal settings, encompassing active learning and Bayesian Experimental Design: here, ICL-derived rewards successfully bound and asymptotically converge to the true learning progress. We corroborate our theory with controlled experiments across continuous and symbolic environments, demonstrating that our ICL-driven framework successfully trains curious data-collection policies that explore optimally.

</details>


### [82] [Insulin4RL: Real-Time Insulin Management in the Intensive Care Unit for Offline Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19481)
*Thomas Frost,Steve Harris*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的离线强化学习（ORL）在医疗应用中往往依赖时间离散化的固定间隔数据，这扭曲了复杂的临床场景，限制了回顾性评估的泛化能力。因此需要一个能反映真实临床采样特征的医疗 ORL 数据集。

Method: 基于 MIMIC-IV 数据库构建，保留了临床数据的非规则时间采样特性。通过提供包含 375,000 条决策轨迹的标准化数据集，引入无模型离线强化学习基准，并采用拟合 Q-评估 (Fitted Q-evaluation) 协议进行评估。

Result: 成功发布了 Insulin4RL 数据集，涵盖 12,209 名 ICU 患者的胰岛素输注决策，并建立了标准化的模型评估基准和评估协议。

Conclusion: Insulin4RL 弥补了现有离线强化学习在医疗数据处理上的局限性，为研究真实临床场景下的模型性能提供了标准化的基准，并指出了未来在处理非规则时间序列医疗数据方向上的研究潜力。

Abstract: Offline reinforcement learning (ORL) offers the potential to improve the quality of clinical decision-making using historical electronic health record (EHR) data. Current training and evaluative practices in this field rely heavily on EHR datasets that have been temporally discretised into fixed, regular time intervals. Discretisation creates fictional representations of complex clinical scenarios and compromises the generalisability of retrospective model evaluations. In this paper, we introduce Insulin4RL, a healthcare ORL dataset featuring naturally irregular inputs and actions from real clinical trajectories. Derived from MIMIC-IV, Insulin4RL comprises over 375,000 labelled decisions across 12,209 patients requiring insulin infusion titration in the Intensive Care Unit. The dataset can thus be used for research into ORL model performance under realistic clinical sampling assumptions. We provide a description of the dataset's structure and characteristics, baseline performance metrics using model-free offline reinforcement learning, and a standardised evaluation protocol using fitted Q-evaluation. We conclude with suggested areas for future research that could be addressed using this resource.

</details>


### [83] [Concept Flow Models: Anchoring Concept-Based Reasoning with Hierarchical Bottlenecks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19489)
*Ya Wang,Adrian Paschke*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了概念流模型（CFM），通过层次化的决策树结构取代传统概念瓶颈模型，在保证模型预测精度的前提下，有效抑制了信息泄露并大幅提升了可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的概念瓶颈模型（CBM）通过利用视觉-语言模型减少了人工标注需求，但随着概念数量的增加，模型极易产生信息泄露，导致其利用虚假或语义无关的相关性进行预测，从而削弱了模型的可解释性。

Method: 1. 提出概念流模型（CFM），利用分层决策树替代传统的扁平瓶颈结构；2. 构建基于视觉嵌入的决策层级，将语义概念分布在各层级中；3. 采用概率树遍历方法训练可微的概念权重，使得模型在推理过程中逐步缩小决策范围。

Result: 在多个基准测试上的实验表明，CFM不仅能达到与扁平CBM相当的预测性能，还能通过减少有效的概念使用量显著降低信息泄露。此外，CFM生成的逐步决策流程为复杂分类任务提供了更清晰、可审计的推理路径。

Conclusion: 概念流模型（CFM）通过引入层次化的决策树结构，有效地解决了传统概念瓶颈模型（CBM）在处理大量概念时产生的信息泄露问题。该方法在保持预测性能的同时，通过分层决策路径提供了更高的透明度和可审计性，为可解释人工智能的发展提供了一种更具鲁棒性的新范式。

Abstract: Concept Bottleneck Models (CBMs) enhance interpretability by projecting learned features into a human-understandable concept space. Recent approaches leverage vision-language models to generate concept embeddings, reducing the need for manual concept annotations. However, these models suffer from a critical limitation: as the number of concepts approaches the embedding dimension, information leakage increases, enabling the model to exploit spurious or semantically irrelevant correlations and undermining interpretability. In this work, we propose Concept Flow Models (CFMs), which replace the flat bottleneck with a hierarchical, concept-driven decision tree. Each internal node in the hierarchy focuses on a localized subset of discriminative concepts, progressively narrowing the prediction scope. Our framework constructs decision hierarchies from visual embeddings, distributes semantic concepts at each hierarchy level, and trains differentiable concept weights through probabilistic tree traversal. Extensive experiments on diverse benchmarks demonstrate that CFMs match the predictive performance of flat CBMs, while substantially mitigating information leakage by reducing effective concept usage. Furthermore, CFMs yield stepwise decision flows that enable transparent and auditable model reasoning with hierarchical class structures.

</details>


### [84] [Algebraic Dead Directions in LayerNorm Transformers: A Forward-Pass-Only Diagnostic at LLM Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19491)
*Tejas Pradeep Shirodkar,P. J. Narayanan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种仅通过LayerNorm的参数即可直接识别Transformer网络“死方向”的代数方法，无需进行任何前向或后向传播，极大地降低了分析奇异结构和模型归一化机制的计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预训练Transformer通常位于损失函数的奇异极小值附近，在该处Fisher信息度量沿“死方向”退化。现有定位死方向的方法（如特征分解或采样）计算成本高昂，且难以仅从参数本身获取信息。因此，作者旨在寻找一种仅依赖网络参数、计算成本极低的死方向定位方法，以深入探索Transformer的内部结构特性。

Method: 研究人员利用LayerNorm的仿射参数$\gamma$，构造出其逆尺度方向$\gamma^{-1}/||\gamma^{-1}||$，并证明了该方向在数学上精确对应于后层归一化激活协方差矩阵的核（kernel）。通过对比14个预训练模型（包括LayerNorm和RMSNorm），验证了该方法在无需前向传递计算下，能准确预测模型参数空间中的死方向。

Result: 实验表明，在LayerNorm模型中，预测的方向与通过一次前向传播测量的最低奇异方向在随机初始化时吻合度高达四位小数，而在RMSNorm模型中该方向不存在（证实了该机制依赖于均值减法投影）。训练后，该方向的协方差特征值会显著下降，证实了死方向的演化特性。此外，该发现还能解释残差流中最小奇异值的块间保留现象，并能仅根据参数分类模型的归一化方式。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了LayerNorm变换器中存在一个由尺度参数直接定义的参数空间“死方向”（dead direction）。这一发现无需前向传播或特征分解即可定位，为理解变换器的奇异极小值结构、模型初始化状态与训练后状态的差异，以及归一化机制对网络动力学的影响提供了精确的代数工具。

Abstract: Pretrained transformers sit near singular minima of the loss, where the Fisher information metric degenerates along dead directions: directions in parameter space along which the directional Fisher vanishes. Locating such a direction normally needs a forward pass and an eigendecomposition of activations, or a sampling-based complexity estimate; none returns a direction computable from the network's parameters alone. We give one, for LayerNorm transformers. The inverse-scale direction $γ^{-1}/\|γ^{-1}\|$ of the LayerNorm affine is an exact algebraic kernel of the post-final-norm centred activation covariance, for any input distribution, and induces a corresponding dead direction in parameter space. It is read from the LN scale parameter alone, with no forward or backward pass and no eigensolve: the cheapest dead-direction read, specific to LayerNorm. We test it on $14$ pretrained transformers ($9$ LayerNorm, $5$ RMSNorm; $160$M-$35$B; language and vision objectives). At random initialisation the predicted direction matches the measured bottom singular direction (one forward pass, direct SVD) to four decimal places on $9/9$ LayerNorm models, and is correctly absent on $5/5$ RMSNorm models, which lack the mean-subtraction projector that creates it. On the trained checkpoint the covariance eigenvalue along this direction deepens by ${\sim}10^3\times$ and further dead directions open; the random-init-to-trained gap is a one-forward-pass, per-checkpoint readout of singular structure along the predicted coordinate. Two consequences follow in closed form: the residual stream's smallest singular value is preserved block-to-block on $13/14$ transformers measured on their own input distribution, the one exception (Gemma$4$-$31$B) a genuine dead direction the same read pinpoints; and the kernel direction's presence classifies a transformer's normalisation from the parameters alone.

</details>


### [85] [Calibrating Generative Models to Feature Distributions with MMD Finetuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19496)
*Nathaniel L. Diamant,Brian L. Trippe*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对生成模型难以匹配目标数据集特征分布的问题，作者提出了 kCGM 方法。通过引入 MMD 最小化和 KL 正则化，kCGM 能够在无需完整数据集训练的情况下，高效地将预训练模型调整为符合特定领域特征分布的要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成模型虽然能产生合理的单个样本，但往往难以匹配目标数据集的特定特征分布。现有的直接微调方法容易导致过拟合且难以精确控制特征匹配，因此需要一种能有效校准特征分布且保持模型泛化能力的方法。

Method: 提出了核校准生成模型 (kCGM)，核心方法是最小化生成分布与目标特征分布之间的最大均值差异 (MMD)，并利用无偏分数函数估计器进行优化，同时引入 KL 正则化以确保模型不偏离预训练模型的原始分布。

Result: 在抗生素分子生成任务中，kCGM 在匹配目标特征分布的同时，比直接微调方法保留了更高的化学有效性；此外，该方法在蛋白质和 DNA 生成任务中也展现了出色的效果，能够有效适配自回归模型及连续/离散扩散模型。

Conclusion: kCGM 通过在特征层面进行分布校准，成功解决了生成模型在特定目标数据集上分布不匹配的问题，且在保持生成质量的同时避免了过拟合，具备良好的跨模态（分子、蛋白质、DNA）通用性。

Abstract: Generative models can produce individually plausible samples while deviating substantially from a target set in the distribution of key features. For example, a model pretrained on broad drug-like chemical space may generate molecules whose molecular features differ from those of a therapeutic class of interest, such as known antibiotics. Correcting such distributional miscalibration is challenging: direct finetuning on the target set can overfit and does not control which features are matched. To fill this gap, we introduce kernel Calibrating Generative Models (kCGM). kCGM minimizes a maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) between generated and target feature distributions using an unbiased score-function estimator, with KL regularization to remain close to the pretrained model. On a target set of 174 antibiotics, direct finetuning sacrifices chemical validity for feature-distribution matching, whereas kCGM improves target feature matching while increasing validity. We further demonstrate kCGM in protein and DNA generation tasks, showing it can adapt autoregressive, continuous-space diffusion, and discrete diffusion models using only feature-level supervision. Code is available at https://github.com/smithhenryd/cgm.

</details>


### [86] [Interactive Pareto navigation for deep multi-task learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19521)
*Augustina C. Amakor,Konstantin Sonntag,Sebastian Peitz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多任务学习中多目标权衡难、计算开销大的痛点，本文提出了一种基于预测-校正和 Krylov 子空间法的交互式探索框架 (PPE)，实现了在兼顾计算效率的同时，根据决策者偏好高效探索 Pareto 最优解流形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多任务学习中，目标数量增加导致计算资源需求剧增且难以平衡；传统的加权求和方法无法有效体现决策者的偏好，且在深度学习场景下多次调整权重计算的开销巨大。因此，需要一种能够结合决策者偏好并高效处理 Pareto 前沿的交互式探索方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为“偏好 Pareto 探索”（Preference Pareto Exploration, PPE）的框架。该方法采用预测-校正（predictor-corrector）机制：预测步骤沿着 Pareto 最优解流形与决策者偏好相切的方向进行移动；校正步骤则通过调整寻找新的最优权衡解。为避免显式计算 Hessian 矩阵，该方法利用 Krylov 子空间法，仅依赖自动微分提供的矩阵-向量乘积，从而大幅提升了计算效率。

Result: 实验结果表明，PPE 框架能够在各种玩具问题和复杂的深度学习任务中有效地导航 Pareto 流形。该方法不仅能够准确反映决策者的偏好，而且通过避免显式的 Hessian 计算，在计算开销上表现出极高的效率与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: PPE 框架通过结合预测-校正方法与 Krylov 子空间技术，成功解决了多目标学习中权衡选择困难及计算成本高昂的问题。它在保持计算效率的同时，为决策者提供了灵活且直观的 Pareto 前沿探索机制，不仅适用于理论分析，也具有极高的深度学习实际应用价值。

Abstract: In multi-task learning, handling an increasing number of objectives can quickly become challenging, both in terms of the computational resources and the decision maker's capacity to choose appropriate trade-offs. A widely used approach is thus to aggregate the individual losses in a single loss function by a weighted sum. This often fails to capture either the decision maker's preferences as a result of the shape of the Pareto front, or requires multiple adjustments and computations which becomes prohibitively expensive in deep learning applications. To address these issues, we introduce a novel framework, Preference Pareto Exploration (PPE), which enforces the decision maker's preferences while accounting for the geometry of the Pareto set in an interactive exploration process. PPE is based on a predictor-corrector method that performs predictor steps tangential to the manifold of Pareto-optimal solutions, following the decision maker's preference. The subsequent corrector step results in a new trade-off reflecting this preference. To avoid explicit Hessian computations when characterizing the tangent space of the manifold, we employ a Krylov subspace method that relies solely on matrix-vector products. These products can be efficiently obtained via automatic differentiation, ensuring both efficiency and robustness throughout the optimization process. The method's functionality and performance are demonstrated using both toy problems and examples from deep learning.

</details>


### [87] [Techniques for Peak Memory Reduction for LoRA Fine-tuning of LLMs on Edge Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19528)
*Hassan Dbouk,Matthias Reisser,Prathamesh Mandke,Likhita Arun Navali,Christos Louizos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一套针对消费级硬件的LoRA微调优化框架，通过量化、高效检查点、Softmax近似等技术，在不损耗性能的前提下大幅降低了微调所需的内存峰值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在终端设备上通过LoRA对大模型进行个性化微调时，内存占用（尤其是长上下文训练时）往往超过硬件限制，现有方案难以平衡内存效率与模型性能。

Method: 提出了四种互补的内存优化技术：1. 基座模型量化与即时反量化；2. 结合选择性激活缓存与磁盘卸载的内存高效检查点技术；3. 基于语义相关令牌子集的Softmax近似；4. Logits掩码技术。

Result: 在Llama-3.2 3B和Qwen-2.5 3B模型上的实验表明，该方法最高可减少26倍至28倍的峰值内存占用，且未牺牲模型性能。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一套高效的LoRA微调内存优化方案，通过多种技术的协同，显著降低了在消费级硬件上微调大模型所需的内存峰值，使得在有限资源设备上微调长上下文大模型成为可能。

Abstract: Fine-tuning of Large Language Models (LLMs) using Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) on an end-user's data offers personalized experiences while keeping data private, but faces severe memory constraints on consumer hardware. Peak memory during fine-tuning often exceeds device limits, especially for models with billions of parameters and long-context training data. This paper introduces a suite of complementary techniques to reduce memory footprint without sacrificing model quality: (1) base model quantization with on-the-fly dequantization, (2) memory-efficient checkpointing combining selective activation caching and disk offloading, (3) softmax approximation using semantically relevant token subsets, and (4) logits masking. Experiments on Llama-3.2 3B and Qwen-2.5 3B demonstrate up to $26\times$ and $28\times$ reduction in peak memory, enabling fine-tuning on resource-constrained devices.

### [88] [Tracking Representation Dynamics in Large Language Models with Persistent Homology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19542)
*Naman Malhotra,Jay Ambadkar,Abhinav Gupta,Kushal Kasivel,Abbas Schwarz,Kamillo Ferry,Anthea Monod*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究利用持久同调分析了LLM在对齐过程中的内部表征演变，发现拓扑结构主要在训练初期发生剧烈重组并迅速稳定，且不同对齐目标会留下独特的“拓扑足迹”，为理解模型行为提供了超越行为评估的深度视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用持久同调（Persistent Homology）技术跟踪大语言模型在有监督微调（SFT）过程中激活空间的拓扑结构变化，通过对1B到7B规模的四个模型进行高密度检查点分析，对比三种不同对齐目标（有用性、无害性及混合训练数据）下的表征演化模式。

Result: 研究发现：1. 大多数拓扑重组发生在训练初期；2. 模型在微调初期表现出短暂的拓扑活动高峰，随后迅速稳定；3. 不同的对齐目标会产生可区分的拓扑轨迹；4. 指令微调模型与预训练模型展现出本质上不同的演化模式。

Conclusion: 持久同调（Persistent Homology）是分析大语言模型对齐过程中内部表征演变的一种有效且互补的工具。研究表明，对齐过程并非线性平稳，而是在初期经历剧烈的拓扑重组后迅速趋于稳定，且不同训练目标会塑造不同的拓扑演化轨迹，这些变化在宏观行为指标中往往难以察觉。

Abstract: Large language models are commonly aligned through supervised fine-tuning, yet little is known about how their internal representations evolve during this process. We study alignment dynamics using persistent homology by tracking the topology of activation spaces throughout fine-tuning. Across four transformer language models ranging from 1B to 7B parameters and three alignment objectives corresponding to helpful, harmless, and mixed training data, we find that the majority of topological reorganization occurs during the earliest stages of training. A dense checkpoint analysis reveals a transient peak in topological activity followed by rapid stabilization. We further show that different alignment objectives induce distinguishable topological trajectories, while instruction-tuned and pretrained models exhibit qualitatively different patterns of evolution. Our results suggest that persistent homology provides a complementary perspective on alignment, revealing representation-level changes that are not apparent from behavioral metrics alone.

### [89] [Predicting Mergeability of Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning Updates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19549)
*Lin Tang,Wei Zhang,Jing Li,Hongyu Chen,Ming Zhao,Yuxuan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究提出MergeProbe工具，通过分析训练初期的梯度与权重对齐情况，在训练完成前即可精准预测LoRA适配器合并后的表现，从而优化模型适配器的合并策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LoRA适配器合并往往要在训练完成后才能评估效果，容易出现“孤立表现良好但合并后冲突”的问题，导致计算资源浪费；研究旨在解决这种昂贵的后期反馈，寻求在训练初期即预测合并的可行性。

Method: 研究提出了MergeProbe预测器，通过分析训练初期（前几个百分点）的低秩更新与梯度在任务间的对齐程度，以及对共享表示的干扰程度，来预测适配器的合并性能；并基于这些信号实现直接合并、重加权、剪枝或路由等决策。

Result: 在MERGE-PEFT基准测试中，MergeProbe在平均和最差情况下的性能保留率均优于现有的抗干扰合并基线，同时相比全任务路由方案，显著降低了部署开销。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了LoRA适配器合并的可预测性，通过MergeProbe这一轻量级工具，可以将合并决策从后期的工程尝试前置到训练初期，从而有效降低因合并导致的性能损耗，为大模型的高效适配器管理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation (LoRA) makes it cheap to train many domain- and task-specific language model adapters, but whether two adapters can be merged is usually discovered only after both have been fully trained and evaluated. This late feedback is costly: adapters that are strong in isolation can interfere destructively once their updates are combined. We ask whether this outcome can be anticipated. We formalize adapter mergeability as the degree to which an adapter preserves its single-task utility after merging, and show that it can be forecast from signals measured in the first few percent of training -- chiefly how the low-rank updates and their gradients align across tasks and how much they disturb shared representations. We package these signals into MergeProbe, a lightweight predictor that estimates pairwise and set-level retention and turns the estimate into a concrete decision: merge directly, reweight, prune, or route. On MERGE-PEFT, a five-domain benchmark spanning math, code, science, instruction following, and safety, MergeProbe attains the best average and worst-case retention among strong interference-aware merge baselines while adding far less deployment overhead than full task routing. This turns LoRA merging from a post-hoc engineering step into an anticipatory measurement problem.

### [90] [Displacement Is Not Direction: Evaluating Fidelity Metrics for Quantized LLM Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19558)
*Miloš Nikolić,Ali Hadi Zadeh,Enrique Torres Sanchez,Andreas Moshovos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究表明，KL散度等保真度指标在评估量化大模型时存在局限性；虽可反映宏观趋势，但在高性能模型的“静默区”内失效，且难以预测具体任务的成败，不能简单地替代基准测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在人工智能开发实践中，通常使用KL散度等保真度指标作为基准测试的低成本代理。本文旨在质疑并实证评估这一实践的有效性，特别是当模型性能接近高精度参考模型时的表现。

Method: 研究人员在Qwen3.6-35B-A3B（28个量化版本）和Devstral-Small-2-24B（41个量化版本）上进行测试，评估了KL散度等保真度指标与下游基准测试分数的相关性。实验涵盖了14种测量变体，包括不同的KL聚合方式、困惑度公式、Top-1一致性等，并在LiveCodeBench上测试了其在代码任务中的失败预测能力和跨模型路由能力。

Result: 实验发现，虽然KL散度在整个队列中与基准分数呈强相关，但在接近基准的“静默区”内，相关性完全消失。此外，在单条提示词层面，KL散度预测任务失败的能力微弱，且无法有效作为跨模型路由指标。分析表明，KL散度主要衡量的是与参考模型的分歧总量，而非分歧的方向性或语义正确性。

Conclusion: 尽管基于KL散度等保真度指标在宏观模型量化评估中表现出相关性，但在模型性能接近基准的“静默区”内，这些指标失效，无法作为衡量模型质量的可靠代理，且在预测具体任务失败或跨模型路由方面表现不佳。研究建议开发者在模型优化和评估中需谨慎使用此类低成本指标。

Abstract: Fidelity metrics, such as per-token KL divergence (KLD) against a high-precision reference, are often used in practice as low-cost proxies for benchmark quality. We test this practice on a 28-quant cohort of Qwen3.6-35B-A3B and a 41-quant cohort of Devstral-Small-2-24B, evaluated across a suite of downstream benchmarks. We find that KLD is strongly correlated with benchmark score over the full cohort ($ρ=-0.72$ on Qwen and $ρ=-0.86$ on Devstral, both with $p<0.001$). However, this relationship collapses to non-significance in the near-baseline silent zone ($ρ=+0.00$ on Qwen and $ρ=-0.24$, $p=0.36$, on Devstral). This collapse persists across 14 measurement variants, including different KLD aggregations, perplexity formulations, top-1 agreement, calibration corpora, and context lengths. At the per-prompt level, KLD has only weak failure-prediction power on code, with failed-vs-passed geometric-mean ratios in $[1.08,1.22]$ across five models on LiveCodeBench, and fails as a cross-model router, achieving only $42.3\%-49.4\%$ accuracy on disagreement prompts. We trace the collapse to a structural decomposition: KLD primarily measures the volume of disagreement with the reference, with silent-zone composite $ρ=+0.94$ ($p<0.001$) on Qwen and $+0.55$ ($p=0.03$) on Devstral, while its relationship to the direction of those disagreements is weak and task-conditional.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究通过对流感样疾病监测及流感相关住院数据进行系统性评估，涵盖了时间与空间泛化设置，对比了经典神经网络、数值型Transformer、预训练时间序列基础模型以及基于大语言模型（LLM）的预测架构。核心方法包括构建了一个融合多种预训练预测器的混合专家（MoE）模型，并探讨了住院数据作为辅助协变量和预训练源的作用。

Conclusion: 本研究为流感预测提供了重要的实证指导：混合专家模型（MoE）通过融合多种预训练模型表现最佳；数值型Transformer架构优于LLM类方法；且在预训练领域与流感动力学机制一致时，预训练效果最为显著。此外，合理利用住院数据作为辅助信号可增强预测的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Seasonal influenza infects millions of people and causes substantial morbidity and mortality in the United States each year, making accurate short-term forecasting a core public-health need. We address this gap through a systematic evaluation of regional influenza forecasting using influenza-like illness surveillance and influenza-associated hospitalization time series under both temporal and spatial generalization settings for 1-4-week-ahead prediction. We compare classical neural network architectures, numerical transformer-based models, pretrained time series foundation models, and LLM-based forecasting approaches. Across tasks, we demonstrate that a mixture-of-experts model that fuses multiple pretrained forecasters achieves the strongest overall performance, indicating that heterogeneous pretrained representations provide complementary predictive information. Our results further show that numerical transformer-based models produce reliable forecasts, while pretraining provides the largest gains at longer horizons, particularly when the pretraining domain is mechanistically aligned with influenza dynamics. In contrast, LLM-based time series methods underperform relative to numerical forecasters in this setting. Finally, we examine hospitalization information as both an auxiliary covariate and a pretraining source. Hospitalization signals provide complementary improvements in selected settings and clarify when additional surveillance streams enhance the robustness of multi-horizon forecasting. These findings provide actionable guidance on model selection, pretraining strategy, and auxiliary-signal use for influenza preparedness.

### [92] [Advances in Scientific Machine Learning for Coupled Fluid Flow and Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19562)
*Gabriel F. Barros,Rômulo M. Silva,Alvaro L. G. A. Coutinho*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文综述了利用科学机器学习（SciML）处理复杂流体动力学问题的研究进展，重点讨论了利用PINNs和β-VAEs等技术构建高效代理模型，以在降低计算成本的同时实现对非线性耦合流体系统的高精度模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不可压缩纳维-斯托克斯方程及标量传输方程所描述的耦合流体流动和传输现象具有强非线性耦合和多尺度特性，导致高保真模拟的计算成本极高。为了应对这一挑战，研究旨在探索利用科学机器学习（SciML）构建高效代理模型，以降低计算复杂度。

Method: 该研究综述了多种SciML方法，包括：1. 基于奇异值分解（SVD）的线性降阶技术（如动态模态分解DMD）；2. 非线性神经网络方法（物理信息神经网络PINNs和β-变分自编码器β-VAEs）；3. 结合高性能计算策略，如自适应网格细化/粗化（AMR/C）和科学浮点数据压缩。此外，通过PINNs对浑浊流进行代理建模，以及利用β-VAEs提取热流中的解耦非线性模态。

Result: 本研究展示了SciML在流体模拟中的应用潜力，通过对锁交换流和瑞利-贝纳德对流等典型基准测试的验证，证明了代理模型能够以显著降低的计算成本实现高精度的近似结果，并成功提取了流场中的物理特征。

Conclusion: 科学机器学习（SciML）为处理复杂流体流动和传输系统提供了一种高效的替代方案。通过结合降维技术、神经网络（如PINNs和β-VAEs）以及高性能计算策略，SciML显著降低了计算成本。虽然其实际应用能力（如实时预测和不确定性量化）仍处于发展阶段，但该方法已证明在特定数据环境下能够实现对复杂耦合系统的快速且准确的近似。

Abstract: This chapter reviews recent advances in Scientific Machine Learning (SciML) for modeling coupled fluid flow and transport phenomena governed by the incompressible Navier-Stokes and scalar transport equations. Such systems, found in applications like turbidity currents and thermal convection, feature strong nonlinear coupling and multiscale behavior that make high-fidelity simulations computationally expensive. To address this, the chapter surveys state-of-the-art SciML methods for building efficient surrogate models, including linear reduced-order techniques based on Singular Value Decomposition (such as Dynamic Mode Decomposition) and nonlinear neural network approaches like Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) and $β$-Variational Autoencoders ($β$-VAEs). It first covers the authors' work combining these models with High Performance Computing strategies, including Adaptive Mesh Refinement/Coarsening (AMR/C) and scientific floating-point data compression. It then presents two new contributions: surrogate modeling of turbidity currents via PINNs, and the extraction of disentangled nonlinear modes from thermal flows using $β$-VAEs. Governing equations and representative benchmarks, including lock-exchange flows and Rayleigh-Bénard convection, illustrate these methodologies. The chapter is intentionally long, covering both the mathematical and physical foundations of coupled fluid flow and the computational aspects of state-of-the-art modeling. Overall, it demonstrates how SciML enables fast, accurate approximations of complex coupled systems within the specific data regimes and modeling assumptions considered, while substantially reducing computational cost relative to full-order simulations. Broader capabilities such as real-time prediction and uncertainty quantification remain active research directions whose feasibility depends strongly on the problem at hand.

### [93] [On the QUEST for Uncertainty Quantification via Highest Density Regions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19569)
*Sam Goring,Tom Kuipers,Nicola Paoletti,David S. Watson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了QUEST方法，通过量化分布高密度区域的体积来衡量不确定性，解决了传统基于评分规则的方法在回归任务中的缺陷，并在理论属性和实验表现上均展现出优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于评分规则（proper scoring rules）的标量不确定性量化方法在回归问题中，当目标统计量非条件期望时往往产生反直觉结果，且在公理化属性上存在不足。

Method: 提出了一种基于勒贝格测度（Lebesgue measure）在分布峰值处集中度的新型不确定性量化方法QUEST，通过引入鲁棒性参数α来量化分布高密度区域的体积，并将其与信息论和经济学中的经典统计量建立了联系。

Result: QUEST在选择性预测基准测试中优于方差和微分熵等标准度量，同时满足了单调性（分布扩展下）和位置平移不变性等重要的不确定性量化公理。

Conclusion: QUEST框架通过关注分布的高密度区域（highest density regions）而非传统的标量风险度量，提供了一种更稳健且符合不确定性量化公理的评估方法，在处理非条件期望目标时表现出显著优势。

Abstract: Uncertainty quantification (UQ) is essential for reliable decision-making in safety-critical applications in probabilistic machine learning. For regression problems, dominant scalar UQ approaches - notably, those based on proper scoring rules - measure uncertainty via pointwise predictive risk. This can lead to counterintuitive results when the target statistic is not the conditional expectation. We propose an alternative framework, in which uncertainty is characterised by the volume of the most probable subset of a distribution's support. QUEST (Quantifying Uncertainty via highest dEnSiTy regions) is a novel approach to UQ based on the concentration of Lebesgue measure at a distribution's peak(s), evaluated at one or more values of a robustness parameter $α$. We establish connections between our measures and classical statistics from information theory and economics. We show that, unlike popular alternatives based on proper scoring rules, QUEST measures of epistemic and aleatoric uncertainty satisfy a set of axioms adapted from the UQ literature, including monotonicity under distributional spread and invariance to location shifts. Selective prediction benchmarks confirm that QUEST performs favourably against standard measures such as variance and differential entropy.

We study the complementary problem of learning a high-level model directly from low-level measurements. Our contributions leverage hypotheses from low-rank causal discovery, and can be summarized as follows: (1) we show that observations generated by a low-rank graph induce latents that form a causal abstraction, (2) we provide identifiability results about these latents, and (3) we propose a practical objective to learn this high-level SCM.

### [95] [IHBench: Evaluating Post-Interruption Recovery in Voice Agents with Structured Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19595)
*Ahmad Salimi,Wentao Ma,Yuzhi Tang,Dongming Shen,Mu Li,Alex Smola*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语音智能体基准测试多关注中断检测与轮次转换的时序问题，忽视了中断发生后的“恢复与响应”能力（如是否回到正确步骤、是否回应用户打断等），导致智能体在实际复杂业务流程中表现不佳。

Method: 引入了IHBench基准测试，涵盖10个企业领域及6种中断类型。采用基于状态机驱动的流程，通过双轴（任务完成度与恢复质量）评估27种音频-语言模型配置，并使用LLM作为裁判与人类评估进行校准。

Result: 闭源模型在中断后的任务完成度与恢复质量上均优于开源模型；随着对话时长增加，闭源模型性能下降速度远低于开源模型；闭源模型在音频与文本模态间表现一致，而开源模型存在明显差距；恢复质量被证实是一个独立于常规对话能力的评估维度。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，中断处理能力是语音智能体在复杂流程中表现的关键维度，且目前闭源模型在该能力上显著优于开源模型。研究验证了基于LLM的自动评估方法与人类评估的一致性，强调了评估中断后恢复质量的必要性。

Abstract: Voice agents deployed in structured workflows (customer service, healthcare scheduling, account management) must handle frequent user interruptions while maintaining progress through multi-step procedures. Existing benchmarks for speech-capable models focus on the timing of interruptions: barge-in detection, endpointing, and turn-taking dynamics. They leave unmeasured what happens after the interruption: does the agent resume the workflow at the correct step? Does it address the user's interjection? Does it avoid re-delivering content the user already heard?
  We introduce IHBench (Interruption Handling Benchmark), a benchmark that evaluates post-interruption recovery in voice agents executing state-machine-driven workflows across 10 enterprise domains. Six interruption types are injected at controlled points mid-utterance, with per-interruption evaluation rubrics generated alongside the data. Each interruption is scored on two axes: task fulfillment and recovery quality.
  We evaluate 27 audio-language model configurations from OpenAI, Google, and the open-weight community. Models vary widely, and recovery quality depends strongly on the interruption type. Across our experiments, closed-weight models are consistently more robust to interruptions than open-weight ones: they win far more often on task fulfillment, degrade roughly 3.3x more slowly as conversations grow longer, and show no audio-versus-text modality gap, whereas the open-weight models lose ground on all three. A human study validates the LLM judge against human annotators, and a cross-benchmark analysis against AudioMultiChallenge indicates that recovery quality is a largely distinct capability axis.

</details>


### [96] [Comparing Linear Probes with Mahalanobis Cosine Similarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19603)
*Zhuofan Josh Ying,Peter Hase,Nikolaus Kriegeskorte*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究证明了“马氏余弦相似度（MCS）”是预测线性探测器分布外（OOD）性能的高效指标，并从理论上解释了其与OOD准确率之间呈现线性关系的根本原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的线性探测器评估通常使用欧几里得余弦相似度，但这种方法忽略了数据分布的特征。研究人员旨在证明考虑测试数据协方差的马氏余弦相似度（MCS）能更好地预测模型在分布外（OOD）数据上的泛化性能，并为这一经验发现提供理论解释。

Method: 该研究通过跨模型、层级和概念领域的实证分析，验证了马氏余弦相似度（MCS）与OOD AUROC之间的强相关性；并基于假设类别投影服从高斯分布，推导并证明了二者均为信噪比（SNR）的Sigmoid函数，从而解释了其线性关系的成因，并确定了该规律失效的边界条件。

Result: 研究证实，在大多数情况下，探测器对参考探测器的MCS与OOD AUROC之间存在近乎完美的线性关系（R^2高达0.98），并成功通过理论推导证明了这种线性关系的本质，同时准确预测了该线性关系在何种条件下会失效。

Conclusion: 马氏余弦相似度（MCS）是衡量线性探测器性能的理论上可靠且经验有效的指标，优于传统的欧几里得余弦相似度。该研究揭示了探测器性能与数据分布特征之间深刻的几何与统计联系。

Abstract: Linear probes are widely used in interpretability research and often compared by cosine similarity. The Mahalanobis cosine similarity (MCS) between two directions, which reweights the inner product by test data covariance, is a natural task-aware refinement. Ying et al. (2026) report that a probe's MCS to a reference probe trained on the out-of-distribution (OOD) data near-perfectly linearly predicts the probe's OOD AUROC (R^2 = 0.98). Here, we extend this empirical finding across models, layers, and concept domains, and prove this general phenomenon in closed form: For balanced classes whose projections are Gaussian, OOD AUROC and MCS to the reference probe are linear because both are sigmoid-shaped functions of the probe's signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) on the test data. The theory also predicts when this linearity fails, which we verify empirically. MCS offers a theoretically grounded and empirically effective alternative to Euclidean cosine similarity for comparing linear probes.

### [97] [Latent Confounded Causal Discovery via Lie Bracket Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19610)
*Sridhar Mahadevan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Kan-Do-Calculus（KDC）的新型因果发现范式，利用干预诱导流的几何属性（如李括号残差）来识别潜变量结构，通过BRIDGE和SKFM两种算法大幅降低了因果模型搜索的复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有因果发现方法在处理潜变量混杂时计算复杂度极高。鉴于Kan-Do-Calculus（KDC）将观察与干预建模为范畴论中的伴随关系，作者旨在利用观测分布与干预分布之间的几何关联（特别是测度导数与局部因果向量场），为存在潜变量的系统开发高效的因果结构发现算法。

Method: 1. BRIDGE算法：结合干预密度比率评估与几何筛选，通过检测李括号（Lie brackets）不闭合导致的弗罗贝尼乌斯残差（Frobenius residuals），识别潜在混杂因素，缩小因果图搜索空间。2. SKFM算法：采用谱流匹配（Spectral Flow Matching）学习摊余干预场，通过谱分解提取潜在曲率，定位直接的李空间终点。

Result: 实验表明，BRIDGE和SKFM两种算法均能有效发现含有潜混杂因子的因果模型，并将可能的DAG（有向无环图）搜索空间规模缩减了多个数量级，验证了该几何范式在复杂因果推断中的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种利用干预诱导流的几何特性来推断潜变量结构的新范式。通过将因果发现转化为几何和微分几何问题，研究成功地在处理潜在混杂因素的同时，显著降低了因果模型搜索的空间复杂度。

Abstract: Recent work on Kan-Do-Calculus (KDC) has established that the boundary between passive observation and active intervention in causal inference is a category-theoretic bi-adjunction, with interventions modeled by left Kan extensions and conditioning by right Kan extensions. This paper introduces two causal discovery algorithms under latent confounding, building on the information-geometric and categorical consequences of KDC. In smooth statistical settings, Radon-Nikodym derivatives between observational and interventional measures induce local causal vector fields; failures of these fields to close under Lie brackets become computable Frobenius residuals, which we interpret as witnesses of failed visible integrability and possible latent or unmodeled structure. Our first algorithm, BRIDGE (Bracket Residuals for Interventional Discovery and Geometric Estimation), combines an interventional density or Radon-Nikodym-ratio engine with a geometric screen that proposes a high-recall family of admissible arrows, identifies non-closing visible pairs as latent-obstruction candidates, and passes the reduced family to downstream score-based or differentiable discovery routines. The second algorithmic contribution, Spectral Kan-Do Flow Matching (SKFM), learns amortized intervention fields and factors latent curvature spectrally, exposing the direct Lie-space endpoint toward which BRIDGE points. A detailed set of experiments show that both algorithms are capable of discovering causal models with latent confounders while collapsing the super-exponential space of possible DAGs by many orders of magnitude. This paper introduces a new paradigm in causal discovery, where latent structure is inferred directly from the geometry of intervention-induced flows.

### [98] [SEAGAN: domain-Specific and Edge-Aware Graph Attention Network for Dynamic Plant Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19623)

Abstract: Graph neural networks (GNNs) provide a flexible framework for learning from scientific data linked through physical, biological, or functional relationships. One promising domain is plant physiology, where measured responses often arise from multiple interacting processes whose exact separation remains difficult even with manual intervention. In plant physiology, a key example is the A-Ci curve, which relates net CO2 assimilation rate (Anet) to leaf intercellular CO2 concentration (Ci) and is used to estimate photosynthetic parameters in leaf and crop-canopy models. However, reliable estimation requires identifying the active biochemical limitation state at each curve point, which remains a major source of uncertainty. Here, we formulate limitation-state identification along A-Ci curves as a graph-based node classification problem, with curve points as nodes. Domain-specific graph representations are created using distance-based k-nearest-neighbor (kNN) and auxiliary-signal-guided (ASG) connectivity, with edge attributes encoding pairwise relations. Results on a large synthetic dataset with known ground-truth limitation states show that graph-based models improve classification, particularly near biochemical transition regions. The best-performing configuration, SEAGAN (domain-Specific and Edge-Aware Graph Attention Network for Dynamic Plant Processes), integrates process-aware node features, edge attributes, kNN connectivity, and graph attention with weighted cross-entropy loss, achieving an F1-score of 0.857 and an accuracy of 0.882. ### [100] [Hard or Just Unreached? Diagnosing the Sampling Blind Spot in Math-Reasoning Difficulty Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19636)
*Luca Zhou,Sajel Shah,Emanuele Rodolà,Roberto Dessì*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 数学推理基准测试中常用的pass@k评估指标存在重大缺陷，未能反映模型在复杂问题上的真实潜力。研究通过激活植入技术发现，许多被 pass@k 标记为无法解决的问题，实际上可以通过特定路径引导在模型内部被正确求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的数学与科学推理基准测试主要依赖pass@k指标作为评估难度信号，然而研究者发现该指标在极具挑战性的任务层级上存在严重的“盲区”，导致许多模型实际上有能力解决但被误判为无法解决的问题。该研究旨在揭示并量化这一缺陷，探讨模型内部表示的潜能。

Method: 该研究引入了一种名为“激活植入（activation grafting）”的诊断与多样化工具。研究者在贪婪解码的基础上，对残差流（residual stream）施加五种廉价的扰动，构成一个六链确定性机制。通过对比这一机制与传统六次采样（pass@6）在GSM8K和MATH数据集上的表现，量化了传统评估指标的盲区，并验证了不同扰动在机制上的显著差异性。

Result: 实验结果显示，在所测试的八个数学数据集单元中，有10.3%至22.9%的问题在常规采样（pass@6）中无法解决，但通过激活植入的六链确定性机制却能成功求解。相比之下，单纯的贪婪解码最多仅能解决6%的此类问题。这证实了所谓的“零命中率”样本层级实际上在模型内部残差流中是结构性可识别的。

Conclusion: 研究指出，现有的数学推理评估指标（pass@k）无法全面衡量模型的推理能力，存在“盲区”。通过激活植入（activation grafting）诱导的确定性多链路径能够解决许多被标记为“无法解决”的问题，证明这些问题在模型内部表示中是结构性可识别的，而非单纯的随机探索失败。这对未来提升模型推理能力及改进评估机制具有重要启示。

Abstract: Math and science reasoning benchmarks rely on pass@k, the fraction of sampled chains that reach gold, as the canonical per-example difficulty signal. The same signal drives RL with verifiable rewards, math data curation, synthetic curricula, and verifier training. We show this proxy has a persistent blind spot on its hardest stratum: on the eight free-form math cells we test (GSM8K and MATH across four open-weight models), 10.3-22.9% of the examples that no sampling seed solves in six tries are instead solved at matched compute by a six-chain deterministic regime. These are greedy decoding plus five cheap residual-stream perturbations applied via activation grafting, while greedy alone solves at most 6% on these math cells. Recovery scales with the additional budget, across perturbations whose mechanistic distinctness we verify across all twelve cells (cross-kind fix-set Jaccard <= 0.47 in every setup). Activation grafting is used as an intervention on internal representations, not a decoding method; we use it purely as a diagnostic and diversification tool, and our recovered items show that the pass@k= 0 % stratum is structurally identifiable in the residual stream rather than that the unmodified model reaches them under ordinary inference.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this work, we introduce a training procedure for shallow neural networks that promotes robustness against adversarial attacks. We solve a non-convex Lipschitz-regularized training program by introducing a convex restriction that can be efficiently solved to global optimality. Our approach can be employed as a post-processing step by taking a pre-trained network as an initial solution to then solving the convex program whose optimal network is guaranteed to be no worse than the initial one. We illustrate the improvements of our training procedure with experiments using real world datasets for regression tasks under an adversarial setting. We show numerically that solving our proposed convex program yields networks with lower objective values on the Lipschitz-regularized program compared to existing methods. Additionally, we show that on certain datasets, networks obtained using our convex training program are both more accurate and robust with respect to adversarial attacks.

### [102] [LOKI: Memory-Free Null-Space Constrained Lifelong Knowledge Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19679)
*Masih Eskandar,Miquel Sirera Perelló,Stratis Ioannidis,Jennifer Dy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对终身知识编辑中存在的模型灵活性不足及依赖历史数据的问题，本文提出了 LOKI 方法，通过动态选择层与梯度零空间投影技术，在无需历史数据的前提下显著提升了模型更新的准确性与稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的终身知识编辑方法存在两大局限：一是固定层更新策略缺乏灵活性且易导致灾难性遗忘；二是通常依赖于访问历史知识或进行繁琐的数据预处理以获取统计信息。

Method: 提出了 LOKI 框架：1. 利用希尔伯特-施密特独立性准则（HSIC）实现动态层选择，增强模型适应性；2. 采用梯度投影技术，将参数更新限制在模型权重的零空间（null-space）内，从而在更新新知识的同时有效避免对既往知识的干扰。

Result: 实验结果表明，LOKI 在多项测试任务中均优于现有的编辑方法，在平均准确率上实现了最高 14% 的性能提升。

Conclusion: LOKI 证明了通过结合动态层选择机制与基于零空间投影的约束更新，无需访问过往知识数据即可在终身知识编辑任务中实现高效且稳定的模型更新，显著缓解了灾难性遗忘问题。

Abstract: Lifelong knowledge editing aims to efficiently and sequentially update language models over time, as new knowledge becomes available or when the model makes mistakes, while preserving acceptable performance on past knowledge. One unresolved challenge is that existing methods modify a fixed set of layers for all new knowledge samples, reducing flexibility and increasing catastrophic forgetting. Another is requiring access to previous knowledge and extensive pre-processing to obtain data statistics. To address these challenges, we introduce LOKI, a novel approach that uses dynamic layer selection based on the Hilbert-Schmidt Independence Criterion and projects gradient updates onto the null-space of the model weights, bypassing the requirement for previous knowledge access. We show that LOKI achieves superior performance to existing approaches across a wide variety of experiments, achieving up to a 14\% improvement in average accuracy.

### [103] [Multi-Granular Attention-Driven Reinforcement Learning Framework for Web Intelligent Enhancement Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19690)

### [104] [Efficiently Representing Algorithms With Chain-of-Thought Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19697)
*Yanhong Li,Anej Svete,Ashish Sabharwal,William Merrill*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明了思维链（CoT）Transformer 能够高效模拟 Word RAM 计算模型，打破了原有基于图灵机模拟带来的高昂性能开销限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多基于图灵机模型论证 Transformer 的计算能力，但图灵机在算法分析上效率较低且缺乏直观性。作者旨在探究更能代表实际计算效率的 Word RAM 模型是否能被 CoT Transformer 高效模拟，以弥补理论与算法实践之间的差距。

Method: 研究人员在三种 Transformer 设置下（有限精度的硬注意力机制、连续向量推理的 CoT，以及结合线性 RNN 的混合架构）构建了模拟机制，将 Word RAM 算法的执行步骤转化为 Transformer 的推理过程，并通过多项式对数开销分析证明了其模拟的高效性。

Result: 研究表明，CoT Transformer 可以在仅有多项式对数开销（poly-logarithmic overhead）的情况下高效模拟任何 Word RAM 算法。在特定简化指令集下，该开销可进一步降至对数级别，远优于此前基于图灵机的模拟方案。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论证明，思维链（CoT）Transformer 能够以极小的多项式对数开销高效模拟 Word RAM 模型。这一发现从算法复杂度层面有力支撑了推理模型在处理复杂计算任务时的可行性，揭示了 Transformer 架构在模拟高效计算模型方面的强大潜力。

Abstract: The increasing popularity of \emph{reasoning} models -- language models that output a series of reasoning or thought tokens before producing an answer -- is justified, in part, by theoretical results showing that chain-of-thought (CoT) transformers can simulate Turing machines, and thus perform arbitrary computation. However, the Turing machine, while suitable for complexity-theoretic analysis, is not convenient, intuitive, or efficient for discussing algorithms. Algorithms are typically designed and analyzed at a higher level of abstraction, captured by the \emph{Word RAM} model with random-access memory and unit-cost operations on $\bigO(\log n)$-bit words. As a result, Word RAM algorithms can be substantially more efficient than their Turing machine counterparts, raising the question: \emph{Can CoT transformers efficiently simulate Word RAM algorithms?} For instance, can they sort $n$ items in $\bigO(n \log n)$ steps or run Dijkstra's algorithm in $\bigO(E + V \log V)$ steps? We answer affirmatively, up to poly-logarithmic overhead. We first establish this for finite-precision transformers with poly-logarithmic width and rightmost unique hard attention, then strengthen the result to two more practical settings with finite width and log-precision: \emph{continuous} CoT, where reasoning takes the form of vectors rather than tokens, and a \emph{hybrid} architecture in which transformer layers sit atop a recurrent (linear RNN) layer. In all three cases, we find that CoT \emph{can} efficiently simulate any Word RAM algorithm with only a poly-logarithmic overhead in $n$. This overhead reduces to log-square when the Word RAM has a ``flat'' instruction set, and only logarithmic for multiplication-free flat instructions -- in stark contrast to known CoT simulations of Turing machines, which require quadratic overhead over Word RAM.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前深度学习研究过于关注大规模数据集和高复杂度模型，忽略了许多实际应用场景（如机器人、无人机、物联网）仅涉及少量类别的事实，且传统模型选择方法在这些场景下计算成本高昂且效率低下。

Method: 提出了一种基于数据侧属性的分类难度度量方法。该方法通过量化“少类别的独特性”（few-class distinctiveness），直接评估数据集特征，从而在无需反复训练和测试模型的情况下进行高效的模型选择与缩放。

Result: 该指标将模型与数据集的匹配评估速度提升了 6 到 29 倍；通过该方法缩放出的模型在保持同等精度的前提下体积显著减小，例如在移动机器人任务中，模型体积较 YOLOv5-nano 减小了 42%。

Conclusion: 在处理少类别数据集时，通过考虑数据集的固有属性（即“少类别的独特性”）来指导模型选择是切实可行的。这种方法不仅能够显著减少计算资源的浪费，还为资源受限环境下的部署提供了比盲目追求大模型更优的性能与效率平衡。

Abstract: While much effort has focused on developing and benchmarking high-performance neural networks, less attention has been given to how dataset properties, known to practitioners, can guide efficient model selection. Neural models are typically evaluated on datasets with thousands of classes, yet many real-world applications involve fewer than ten. To address this understudied but common setting, we develop a measure of classification difficulty based on data-side properties and show how it enables more efficient model selection for few-class datasets, where traditional approaches are less effective. We term this phenomenon "few-class distinctiveness". Our metric allows comparison of models and datasets 6 to 29$\times$ faster than repeated training and testing. Leveraging this insight, we extend scaled model families below the smallest published models, achieving greater efficiency at similar accuracy, for example models up to 42% smaller than YOLOv5-nano for a mobile robot task. Targeting resource-constrained applications, we demonstrate few-class model selection across mobile robot, drone, and IoT scenarios, highlighting practical gains in efficiency without sacrificing performance.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 DeFog 虽然能缓解离线强化学习中因帧丢失导致的性能下降，但由于其离线学习的特性，难以泛化到训练集之外的新状态。为了解决这一局限性，作者旨在构建一种能够通过实时交互学习，并具备抗丢帧鲁棒性的在线模型。

Method: 该研究提出了 OnDeFog，这是一种结合了 DeFog（针对随机丢帧的决策 Transformer 机制）与 ODT（在线决策 Transformer）的方法。它通过与环境的直接交互进行在线策略学习，并引入了处理丢帧和奖励缺失的特定机制，从而在在线学习的同时具备了应对丢帧的能力。

Conclusion: OnDeFog 通过将 DeFog 的抗丢帧机制与在线决策 Transformer (ODT) 结合，成功解决了离线方法在处理未见状态时的泛化能力不足问题，并提升了强化学习代理在动态丢帧环境下的鲁棒性。

Abstract: In challenging real-world reinforcement learning applications, communication delays or sensor failures often cause frame dropping, in which the agent cannot receive the dropped states and associated rewards. To address the performance degradation caused by frame dropping, the Decision Transformer under Random Frame Dropping (DeFog) was developed by incorporating additional mechanisms into the decision transformer to tackle frame dropping. Although DeFog can mitigate performance degradation in frame-dropping environments, since DeFog is an offline learning method, it struggles to effectively generalize to novel states not adequately represented in the training dataset. In this study, we propose OnDeFog, which integrates the mechanisms in DeFog with the online decision transformer (ODT), an online reinforcement learning method that learns policies through direct environmental interaction. Comprehensive experimental evaluation demonstrates that our proposed OnDeFog achieves superior performance compared to ODT in environments characterized by high dropping frame rate and outperforms DeFog on datasets containing a large amount of low-reward data.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出并分析了联邦双层效用预测（FBPS）问题，开发了两种求解方法：FBi-RRM（在压缩条件下实现线性收敛）和FBi-SGD（基于联邦超梯度估计的通信高效随机优化方法，适用于小灵敏度场景）。

Most existing formulations assume fixed client data distributions, which can be violated by performativity, where deployed decisions reshape client behavior and data collection, inducing client-specific, decision-dependent distribution shift. We study federated bilevel performative prediction, where both upper-level (UL) and lower-level (LL) objectives are evaluated under client-dependent, decision-dependent distributions. We formalize the federated bilevel performatively stable (FBPS) point under a decoupled-risk perspective and provide sufficient conditions for its existence and uniqueness. We then develop two federated methods to compute the FBPS solution: FBi-RRM, which converges linearly under a contraction condition, and FBi-SGD, a communication-efficient stochastic method based on federated hypergradient estimation with convergence guarantees under diminishing step sizes when sensitivities are sufficiently small. ### [108] [Manifold Bandits: Bayesian Curriculum Learning over the Latent Geometry of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19750)
*Darrien McKenzie,Nicklas Hansen,Xiaolong Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了“贝叶斯流形课程”（BMC），通过引入结构感知和任务类型感知，将问题采样视为流形上的贝叶斯决策问题，有效克服了传统强化学习课程方法在处理大模型推理任务时的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自适应课程学习方法通常将问题采样视为独立臂的传统老虎机问题，忽视了任务空间中存在的问题间关联性和结构化异质性，导致无法充分利用大模型学习过程中的潜在表示空间。

Method: 提出了一种名为“贝叶斯流形课程”（Bayesian Manifold Curriculum, BMC）的框架。该方法将问题组织成层级任务树，并利用贝叶斯学习来指导采样，将问题采样建模为带有内源性非平稳性的“流形结构化多臂老虎机”问题。

Result: 实验表明，不同的采样策略在生产力（学习信号）、多样性（任务流形覆盖）和效用（评估相关性）之间存在权衡。相比仅关注难度的策略，BMC框架能够更全面地利用任务空间结构，显著提升模型性能。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，仅依据难度进行采样不足以优化大模型的推理能力。通过将问题空间视为具有流形结构的整体，并结合任务的层级结构和类型感知进行采样，可以更有效地平衡学习效率、任务覆盖率与评估相关性，从而提升大模型的推理性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) is a central approach for improving reasoning capabilities in large language models (LLMs), where training efficiency depends critically on how problems are sampled during optimization. Existing adaptive curriculum learning methods typically prioritize prompts of intermediate difficulty, treating problem selection as a standard bandit problem with independent arms and overlooking the structured, heterogeneous nature of the task space. In this work, we frame problem sampling as a manifold-structured bandit problem with endogenous non-stationarity: problems are related through the model's latent representation space, and sampling decisions can steer how learning signals evolve across that space. To operationalize this perspective, we introduce Bayesian Manifold Curriculum (BMC), a structure-aware framework that organizes problems into a hierarchical task tree and applies Bayesian learning to guide sampling. Empirically, we find that different sampling strategies induce non-trivial tradeoffs between productivity (learning signal), diversity (coverage of the task manifold), and utility (evaluation relevance). These results show that prioritizing difficulty alone is insufficient for strong downstream performance, highlighting the importance of incorporating structure and type-awareness into problem sampling.

### [109] [Learning universal approximations for partial differential equations with Physics-Informed Broad Learning System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19754)
*Zhiwen Yu,Derong Yang,Liujian Zhang,Kaixiang Yang,Peilin Zhan,Jianmin Lv,Jane You,C. L. Philip Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数值求解器计算成本高昂且依赖网格，而现有的物理信息神经网络（PINN）虽无需网格，但存在收敛缓慢和优化不稳定的问题，因此需要一种更高效的求解框架。

Method: 提出了“物理信息广泛学习系统”（PIBLS），该方法将 PDE 求解重构为一种无需反向传播（Backpropagation-free）的直接最小二乘优化问题，并改进了算法以处理非线性 PDE，同时证明了其在该领域具有通用逼近属性。

Abstract: Partial differential equations (PDEs) play a central role in modeling complex physical, biological, and engineering systems. While traditional numerical solvers are robust, they often incur prohibitive computational costs due to mesh dependencies, whereas recent Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) offer a mesh-free alternative but frequently suffer from slow convergence and optimization instability. To bridge this gap, this article proposes the Physics-Informed Broad Learning System (PIBLS), a novel backpropagation-free framework that reformulates PDE solving as a direct least-squares optimization. We improved an algorithm within this framework to handle nonlinear PDEs efficiently and provide a rigorous mathematical proof establishing the universal approximation property of PIBLS for these equations. Experiments on linear and nonlinear PDEs demonstrate that PIBLS is one to three orders of magnitude faster than conventional PINNs while achieving significantly higher solution accuracy. This framework provides a computationally efficient paradigm for scientific machine learning, offering a practical, high-speed alternative for real-time simulation and design optimization tasks.

### [110] [An Information Theoretic Framework for Graph Novelty Generation via Latent Mixture Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19770)
*Itsuki Nakagawa,Kenji Yamanishi*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图生成模型往往关注于模仿现有数据分布，但在生成既具有创新性（与现有模式显著不同）又能保持全局结构一致性的数据方面仍缺乏系统性的方法和理论保障。

Method: 提出一种基于信息论的图新颖性生成框架：1. 将数据嵌入潜在空间并使用有限混合模型建模潜在分布；2. 利用最小描述长度（MDL）原则，将新颖性定义为样本被现有混合组件“难以解释”的程度，并将可靠性定义为样本对整体结构的影响限制；3. 通过设置显式的阈值条件进行样本生成。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在合成和基准图数据集上实现了原则性的新颖性生成，并提供了可量化的风险评估；理论分析证明，在适当的阈值下，误分类非新颖或不可靠样本的概率以明确的速率收敛于零。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种基于信息论的图数据新颖性生成框架，通过最小描述长度原则，在保持全局结构一致性的前提下，实现了具有可量化风险的创新数据生成，为生成模型提供了一种严谨的理论支撑。

Abstract: We propose an information-theoretic framework for graph novelty generation, which aims to generate data that are distinct from existing patterns while preserving global structural consistency. Our approach embeds data into a latent space, models the latent distribution using finite mixture models, and generates novel samples by imposing explicit novelty and reliability conditions formulated in terms of description length. Specifically, novelty is enforced by requiring generated samples to be poorly explained by all existing mixture components, while reliability constrains their impact on the overall mixture structure under the Minimum Description Length (MDL) principle. We provide a theoretical analysis showing that, with appropriate threshold choices, the probabilities of misclassifying non-novel or unreliable samples converge to zero with explicit rates. Experiments on synthetic and benchmark graph datasets demonstrate that the proposed method enables principled novelty generation with quantifiable risk.

### [111] [Flow Map Denoisers: Traversing the Distortion-Perception Plane for Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19802)
*Nicolas Zilberstein,Morteza Mardani,Santiago Segarra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于流映射模型的新方法，通过调节单一的前瞻参数，即可在图像恢复的“失真-感知”权衡曲线上自由切换，无需额外训练，即可在各种图像恢复任务中同时实现高保真度与高质量的感知效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图像恢复领域长期面临“失真-感知”权衡难题：最小化误差的方法往往导致图像模糊，而追求高感知质量的方法则可能损失图像的真实性。现有方法通常需要在两个极端之间做出选择，或者需要昂贵的成对数据监督、辅助模型及复杂的采样参数调优，缺乏一种能够灵活、连续控制该权衡的通用方法。

Method: 该方法基于流匹配（Flow Matching）的扩展——流映射模型，通过学习一个平均场（average field）并引入前瞻参数（lookahead parameter t）作为控制旋钮。该参数能够隐式地定义一个降噪器族，从而在最小均方误差（MMSE）和感知质量之间实现连续跨越。在即插即用（Plug-and-Play）求解框架下，该机制同样适用于各类线性与非线性反问题。

Result: 理论分析验证了在针对高斯目标时，该方法能精确恢复最优DP边界；实验结果在CelebA和AFHQ数据集上的多种反问题（如超分辨率、修复等）中表明，仅需一个预训练模型即可在感知质量与数据一致性之间达成优异的权衡，且表现媲美甚至超越了现有的专用基准模型。

Conclusion: 本文提出的流映射模型（Flow Map Models）证明了通过简单的单参数调整即可在失真-感知（DP）边界上实现连续调节，无需针对特定目标训练多个模型或进行复杂的超参数调优，为图像恢复任务提供了一种统一且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Image restoration faces a fundamental tradeoff: methods that minimize error produce blurry reconstructions, while those that maximize perceptual quality yield sharp but less faithful images. Existing approaches either commit to a single operating point on this distortion perception (DP) frontier or require paired-data supervision, auxiliary models, or hyperparameter tuning of the sampler to access different points. We show that flow map models, a recent extension of flow matching for few-step sampling that learns an average field, implicitly define a one-parameter family of denoisers that continuously spans the DP frontier. The lookahead parameter t acts as a control knob between the MMSE and perceptual regimes. For Gaussian targets, we prove that varying t exactly recovers the optimal DP frontier; for natural images, we observe similar behavior empirically. Within a Plug-and-Play solver, the same mechanism extends to general inverse problems, where it controls a tradeoff between perceptual alignment and data consistency. Despite the lack of exact optimality guarantees in this setting, a single trained flow map spans the DP tradeoff, matching or exceeding specialized baselines at both extremes. Extensive experiments on CelebA ($128\times 128$) and AFHQ ($256\times 256$) across several linear and nonlinear inverse tasks validate our findings.

</details>


### [112] [Uncertainty-Aware Reward Modeling for Stable RLHF](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19818)
*Licheng Pan,Haocheng Yang,Haoxuan Li,Yichen Sun,Yunsheng Lu,Shijian Wang,Lei Shen,Yuan Lu,Zhixuan Chu,Hao Wang*

TL;DR: 针对RLHF中奖励模型缺乏不确定性感知及策略优化放大错误信号的问题，提出UARM框架，通过不确定性校准和优势函数重加权，显著提升了模型对齐的质量与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的RLHF流程存在两大缺陷：奖励模型作为确定性估计器无法感知不确定性，且GRPO等策略优化算法会放大不确定奖励带来的负面影响，导致模型在探索中出现严重的奖励欺骗（Reward Hacking）。

Method: 提出不确定性感知奖励建模（UARM）：1. 利用基于分位数的共形预测（Conformal Prediction）为奖励模型提供校准后的不确定性估计；2. 在GRPO策略优化中引入异方差方差分解（Heteroscedastic Variance Decomposition）对优势函数进行重加权，以降低不可靠奖励信号的权重。

Result: 在HelpSteer、UltraFeedback和PKU-SafeRLHF等数据集上的实验表明，UARM显著提升了奖励模型的校准能力，有效抑制了奖励欺骗，并提升了模型在对齐任务中的最终表现。

Conclusion: UARM通过引入不确定性感知机制，有效解决了RLHF中奖励模型不可靠和策略优化中错误信号被放大的问题，为大模型对齐提供了一种更稳健、更可信的训练范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) aligns large language models by training reward models on preference data and optimizing policies to maximize predicted rewards. However, this pipeline faces two fundamental challenges: (1) reward models cannot signal when their predictions are unreliable, since they usually act as deterministic point estimators; and (2) modern group-based policy optimization can amplify unreliable reward signals, as exemplified by GRPO's uniform treatment of rewards during advantage computation. As policies explore increasingly diverse responses, these two limitations create a critical vulnerability: unreliable reward estimates may be granted disproportionate influence, triggering severe reward hacking. We propose Uncertainty-Aware Reward Modeling (UARM), which equips reward models with calibrated uncertainty via quantile-based conformal prediction and reweights GRPO advantages through heteroscedastic variance decomposition. Experiments across HelpSteer, UltraFeedback, and PKU-SafeRLHF demonstrate that UARM significantly improves reward model calibration, reduces reward hacking, and enhances downstream alignment quality compared to standard GRPO and uncertainty-agnostic baselines.

Specifically, we use proximity graphs--such as Delaunay triangulation, Gabriel graph, k-Nearest Neighbor graph, and Yao graph--as the input for GNNs (including GraphSAGE, Graph Convolutional Networks, and Graph Attention Networks) to perform message passing.

Self-supervised learning can leverage these unlabeled tables, and recent binning-based pretexts offer a promising inductive bias, but existing objectives fix a single global quantile discretization and apply feature-agnostic supervision. We propose Adaptive Binning, a training-adaptive discretization pretext for tabular SSL that couples discretization to learning through a feature-wise coarse-to-fine curriculum. Motivated by the spectral bias of neural networks and the principles of curriculum learning, our method progressively refines discretization per feature upon plateau detection and selects representation-aware splits to jointly improve value-space concentration and representation-space coherence. A heterogeneity-aware objective unifies categorical reconstruction with ordinal supervision for numerical features, and experiments on public medical tabular datasets under unified evaluation protocols show consistent gains for linear probing and fine-tuning without dataset-specific discretization tuning. Our code is available at https://github.com/labhai/Adaptive-Binning.

### [117] [Global Convergence of Gradient Descent for Score Matching in Gaussian Mixtures via Reverse Fisher Divergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19876)
*Alexander Tyurin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过理论分析证明，相比传统的“前向Fisher散度”，使用“反向Fisher散度”优化高斯混合模型能够显著改善优化景观，从而实现从随机初始化出发的全局收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代生成模型（如扩散模型）常用的前向Fisher散度在简单高斯混合模型设置中常出现收敛缓慢或依赖初始化的不良现象。为了寻找更稳健的优化目标，本文探索了反向Fisher散度在优化性能上的潜力。

Method: 本文采用理论分析方法，对比了前向与反向Fisher散度在梯度下降（GD）下的表现。通过Lyapunov分析，推导了学生模型（高斯混合模型）在不同初始化条件下的收敛性质，并分析了模型在不同成分配置下的动力学行为。

Result: 理论分析证明，对于单高斯教师模型，梯度下降可从任意初始化实现全局收敛；对于更复杂的混合高斯教师模型，在满足均值分离假设下，通过随机初始化同样能保证全局收敛，且学生模型组件能有效逼近教师组件，实现总体分布的收敛。

Conclusion: 研究证明，与前向Fisher散度相比，反向Fisher散度在拟合高斯混合模型（GMM）时具有更优越的优化景观。通过梯度下降法，该方法能够从任意或随机初始化出发，实现全局收敛，为生成模型和统计建模提供了更稳健的训练目标选择。

Abstract: The score matching problem is a central training objective in modern generative modeling, diffusion models, fitting unnormalized statistical models, and inverse problems. A standard approach is to minimize the forward Fisher divergence, where the expectation is taken with respect to the teacher distribution. However, recent results show that even in simple Gaussian mixture model settings, this objective can lead to undesirable and initialization-dependent convergence behavior. In this paper, we study an alternative objective: the reverse Fisher divergence, where the expectation is taken with respect to the student distribution. We analyze gradient descent (GD) for fitting Gaussian mixture models and show that this change in the objective leads to significantly better optimization properties. First, when the teacher distribution is a single Gaussian and the student is a Gaussian mixture model with fixed weights and identity covariances, we prove the global convergence of GD from arbitrary initializations. Second, we extend the analysis to the case where the teacher is also a Gaussian mixture model and prove global convergence guarantees under a global random initialization scheme and a $\widetildeΩ(1)$-separation assumption on the target means. In particular, with high probability, each student component converges near its closest teacher component, and we provide conditions under which the student distribution converges in total variation distance. Our proofs rely on a new Lyapunov-based analysis of the gradient descent dynamics, showing that the reverse Fisher divergence has a much more favorable optimization landscape than the forward Fisher divergence.

### [118] [On the Oracle Complexity of Interpolation-Based Gradient Descent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19878)
*Dongmin Lee,William Lu,Anuran Makur*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出PPI-GD算法，通过分段多项式插值近似全梯度，有效利用训练数据的平滑性提升了梯度下降法的预言机复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明，经验风险最小化（ERM）损失函数在训练数据层面的平滑性可以被利用以改进梯度下降（GD）算法的预言机复杂度，但缺乏一种有效的、利用这种平滑性的具体算法框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为分段多项式插值梯度下降（PPI-GD）的不精确梯度方法。该方法通过在数据域的等距点上查询一阶预言机，获取梯度样本，并构建分段多项式插值来近似每次迭代中的全梯度。研究分析了该方法在强凸和非凸损失函数下的预言机复杂度。

Result: 在数据空间维度受限于训练样本数量的多对数函数的情况下，PPI-GD在损失函数足够平滑的关键区域内表现优于多种现有的GD变体。同时，研究将双三次样条插值的误差分析扩展至d元张量积多项式插值领域。

Conclusion: PPI-GD方法为利用训练数据层面的平滑性来降低一阶优化算法的预言机复杂度提供了有效的理论框架，特别是在高维数据空间受限的场景下具有优越性。此外，该研究对张量积多项式插值的误差分析贡献了新的理论工具。

Abstract: Recent work on first-order optimizers for empirical risk minimization (ERM) has suggested that smoothness of ERM loss functions in the training data, rather than in the optimization parameters, can be leveraged to improve the oracle complexity of gradient descent (GD) methods. In this paper, we propose an inexact gradient method, piecewise polynomial interpolation-based gradient descent (PPI-GD), which approximates the full gradient in each iteration by querying the first-order oracle at equidistant points in the data domain to construct polynomial interpolants of the resulting gradient samples over appropriately sized patches of the data domain. We analyze the oracle complexity of PPI-GD for strongly convex and non-convex loss functions when the data space dimension is bounded by a polylogarithmic function of the number of training samples, and find it to outperform several GD variants in key regimes when the loss function is sufficiently smooth. Furthermore, our analysis extends several techniques from the error analysis of bicubic spline interpolants to the setting of $d$-variate tensor product polynomial interpolants which may be of independent interest in interpolation analysis.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的多智能体多臂老虎机模型往往假设智能体是完全理性的，但在实际应用中，人类的决策往往受到行为经济学因素的影响，具有风险敏感性。研究旨在通过累积前景理论（CPT）更准确地刻画人类偏好，并解决在该决策模型下，双边匹配市场中智能体学习效率低下及对抗环境下鲁棒性不足的问题。

Method: 1. 引入累积前景理论（CPT）对奖励进行非线性加权，以模拟人类的风险敏感偏好（使用α-Hölder连续权重函数）；2. 对现有的学习算法进行分析，并针对CPT偏好下的后悔界进行了理论推导；3. 设计了一种优化算法，通过审慎选择主动臂集（Active Set）来改进探索策略；4. 针对对抗性市场环境（奖励受污染），提出了鲁棒性算法，分别处理污染预算已知与未知两种场景。

Result: 1. 在标准CPT设定下，证明了算法的后悔界为 $\mathcal{O}(K\log T (1/Δ)^{2/α})$；2. 通过优化主动臂集策略，消除了后悔界中对于臂数 $K$ 的依赖，在 $K$ 远大于玩家数 $N$ 时实现了最优后悔保证；3. 在存在奖励污染的对抗性市场中，针对已知和未知污染预算两种情况，均获得了对数级的玩家最优后悔界。

Conclusion: 本研究成功将累积前景理论（CPT）引入多智能体多臂老虎机问题，不仅在标准设定下推导出了最优后悔界，还通过主动臂集选择策略克服了传统算法在臂数较多时的局限性，并进一步为对抗性、受污染的市场环境提供了鲁棒性保障，证明了人类偏好建模对强化学习算法优化具有重要意义。

Abstract: We study a multi-agent multi-armed bandit problem in the competitive setup with two-sided matching markets under a human centric decision making model. To capture human preferences, we use cumulative prospect theory (CPT) that weighs the actions of the agent in a nonlinear fashion using a ($α$-Hölder continuous) weight function. CPT has been widely used in behavioral economics and risk sensitive machine learning to emulate human preferences. We analyze the state-of-the-art learning algorithm with CPT weight distorted rewards and obtain a player optimal regret of $\mathcal{O}(K\log T \left(\frac{1}Δ\right)^{2/α})$, where $K$ denotes the number of arms, $T$ is the learning horizon, and $Δ$ represents (suitably defined) players' minimum preference gap. Noticing the dependence on $Δ$ to be sub-optimal, we further improve this regret by judiciously selecting the active set of arms during exploration, which removes the dependence on $K$ in the dominant term and achieves an improved (optimal) regret guarantees in the setting where the number of arms $K$ is significantly larger than the number of players $N$. In addition, we consider adversarial markets where the observed rewards of the agents may be corrupted. We propose and analyze algorithms for robust markets with CPT as risk sensitive measure in both settings where the total corruption budget is known and where it is unknown, and establish logarithmic player-optimal regret guarantees in both cases.

</details>

Abstract: Modeling long-sequence medical time series data, such as electrocardiograms (ECG), poses significant challenges due to high sampling rates, multichannel signal complexity, inherent noise, and limited labeled data. Structured state space models (S4) excel at long-sequence modeling, but existing S4 architectures fail to capture the unique characteristics of multichannel physiological waveforms. In this work, we propose SL-S4Wave, a self-supervised learning framework that combines contrastive learning with a tailored encoder built on structured state space models. The encoder incorporates multi-layer global convolution using multiscale subkernels, enabling the capture of both fine-grained local patterns and long-range temporal dependencies in noisy, high-resolution multichannel waveforms. Extensive experiments on real-world datasets demonstrate that SL-S4Wave (1) consistently outperforms state-of-the-art supervised and self-supervised baselines in a challenging arrhythmia detection task, (2) achieves high performance with significantly fewer labeled examples, showcasing strong label efficiency, and (3) maintains robust performance on long waveform segments, highlighting its capacity to model complex temporal dynamics in long sequences that most existing approaches fail to efficiently model, and (4) transfers effectively to unseen arrhythmia types, underscoring its robust cross-domain generalization. We additionally evaluate SL-S4Wave on multiple EEG tasks, achieving superior performance over strong baselines, demonstrating generalizability of our approach beyond cardiac waveforms.

*Zhuoyu Cheng,Kohei Hatano,Eiji Takimoto*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的强盗优化研究往往假设环境是静态的或满足特定分布，而现实场景中往往存在非凸、非光滑的对抗性扰动。为了更稳健地处理这类复杂环境，本文旨在探讨当损失函数由基础的凸且β-光滑部分与受全局预算限制的对抗性扰动共同组成时，如何实现有效的在线学习和后悔最小化。

Result: 推导出了针对具有全局预算扰动的凸且β-光滑损失函数的期望后悔界，并清晰地刻画了扰动预算对后悔值的影响程度。当扰动项为零时，该结果与标准的强盗凸优化算法的性能一致。

Abstract: We study adversarial bandit optimization in which the loss functions may be non-convex and non-smooth. In each round, the learner selects an action and observes only the loss incurred at that action. The loss consists of an underlying convex and $β$-smooth component and an adversarial perturbation that may be chosen after observing the learner's action. The perturbations are subject to a global budget controlling their cumulative magnitude over time.
  This framework extends the globally budgeted, post-action perturbation model from underlying linear losses to general convex and $β$-smooth losses. For this broader class, we establish expected regret guarantees that explicitly characterize the effect of the perturbation budget.
  To establish these guarantees, we modify a standard bandit optimization algorithm and develop an analysis that controls the additional regret caused by the perturbations. In the absence of perturbations, our results reduce to regret guarantees for the standard bandit convex optimization setting with $β$-smooth losses.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散模型分数逼近理论往往依赖于利普希茨连续性或光滑流形假设，这与现实中感知数据存在奇异点、锐利边界和不连续聚类的特点不符。本文旨在建立一个适用于更广泛、更具一般性分布的通用分数逼近定理。

Method: 作者提出了一种新颖的离散混合（discrete-mixture）公式，并结合ReLU神经网络进行分数函数逼近。通过利用上闵可夫维度（upper Minkowski dimension）来刻画数据结构，证明了模型复杂度仅随该维度而非环境维度呈指数增长。

Result: 建立了一个通用的分数逼近定理，证明了对于任意紧集上支持的分布，可以使用ReLU网络以受控的复杂度（仅与上闵可夫维度 $d$ 指数相关）逼近分数函数，从而打破了环境维度的指数诅咒，并验证了扩散模型处理不规则、非平滑数据结构的能力。

Conclusion: 本文证明了扩散模型在处理具有复杂几何结构（如非平滑、存在奇异点或不连续边界）的现实数据时具有坚实的理论支撑。研究表明，扩散模型能够克服维度灾难，通过ReLU网络实现对任意紧集分布的分数函数的高效逼近。

Abstract: The remarkable success of score-based diffusion models has spurred significant efforts to establish their theoretical foundations. However, existing complexity bounds for score approximation rely heavily on restrictive assumptions like Lipschitz continuous densities or smooth manifold supports, which are routinely violated by the singularities, sharp boundaries, and disjoint clusters inherent to real-world perceptual data. This work establishes a universal score approximation theorem that works for any distribution supported on any compact set of upper Minkowski dimension $d$. Using a novel discrete-mixture formulation, we prove that the score function can be approximated with a ReLU network whose complexity grows exponentially only with $d$, thus breaking the exponential curse of ambient dimensionality. Combined with existing theories on accurately solving the backward diffusion SDE for arbitrary compact distributions, our work shows that diffusion models readily adapt to irregular, non-smooth data structures, explaining their competence in real-world generative tasks.

### [123] [ADaPT: Token-Level Decoupling for Efficient Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19919)
*Tingyun Li,Zishang Jiang,Jinyi Han,Xinyi Wang,Sihang Jiang,Han Xia,Zhaoqian Dai,Shuguang Ma,Fei Yu,Jiaqing Liang,Yanghua Xiao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型长链式推理成本高昂与效率优化导致性能下降的矛盾，ADaPT通过在训练中解耦效率与正确性信号，并引入可控的模式选择标记，实现了推理成本与性能的精确动态平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型为了性能依赖长链式思考，但全局应用导致计算成本过高；而现有的效率优化方法往往通过缩短推理路径来降低成本，却不可避免地损害了模型的推理能力。其核心原因在于训练时未能区分效率目标与正确性目标，导致模型对长但正确的推理过程产生不合理的惩罚。

Method: 提出了自适应双过程思维（ADaPT）框架：1. 在token层面引入“模式选择标记”以显式区分快速思维与慢速思维；2. 在训练中仅对模式选择标记施加效率奖励，从而避免对长链式思考过程的惩罚；3. 在推理阶段，通过调整模式选择标记的生成概率，实现对推理成本与性能的实时连续控制。

Result: 实验表明，ADaPT在多个推理基准测试中，能够在显著降低推理计算成本的同时，维持甚至优化模型原有的强大推理性能，并在推理时表现出良好的效率-性能帕累托前沿控制能力。

Conclusion: ADaPT通过在训练阶段解耦效率激励与正确性优化，并引入模式选择标记，成功实现了推理模型在效率与性能之间的灵活权衡，为构建高效且强推理能力的模型提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Large reasoning models rely on long chain-of-thought to achieve strong performance, but applying such reasoning uniformly incurs high computational cost. Existing efficiency-oriented methods attempt to shorten or mix reasoning strategies, yet often degrade reasoning capability. We identify the root cause as sequence-level coupling between efficiency incentives and correctness optimization, which implicitly penalizes long but correct reasoning trajectories. To address this issue, we propose Adaptive Dual-Process Thinking (ADaPT), a token-level dual-process framework that explicitly decouples efficiency and correctness signals during training. ADaPT introduces a mode-selection token to control fast and slow reasoning, applying efficiency-related rewards exclusively to this token to avoid penalizing correct long reasoning while encouraging efficiency when appropriate. Moreover, ADaPT enables precise and continuous control over the efficiency-performance trade-off at inference time: by adjusting the generation probability of the mode-selection token, a single trained model can smoothly move along the efficiency-performance Pareto frontier. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ADaPT significantly reduces inference cost while maintaining strong reasoning performance across multiple benchmarks.

### [124] [Compositionality Emerges in a Narrow Depth-Connectivity Regime: Architecture Constraints and Solution Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19941)
*Dat H. Do,Rushi Shah,Duc V. Le,Dianbo Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了组合性在神经网络中的涌现机制，指出其仅在特定的稀疏连接和深度配置下才会被梯度下降发掘。通过相似度剪枝和深度预测，可以有效引导模型形成具有组合性的内部表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组合性被认为是实现泛化的基础，但标准梯度下降训练的模型往往难以自发形成组合性内部结构。研究者旨在探讨组合性涌现的条件，以及模型为何在某些情况下会收敛到非组合性的解，从而寻找诱导模型产生组合性的方法。

Method: 1. 实验探索：在不同深度和连接稀疏度下训练模型，观察组合性的涌现情况。
2. 相似度剪枝（Similarity-based Pruning, SP）：一种恢复组合性连接结构的算法。
3. 启发式深度预测器：用于预估模型在何种深度配置下最易形成组合性。
4. 理论框架：结合组合稀疏性、体积比论证及特征干扰界，从数学上解释为什么组合性解仅存在于特定的“深度-连接”区间内。

Result: 1. 组合性并非总是出现，而是存在于特定的“连接-深度”甜蜜点（sweet spot）。
2. 在连接维度上，组合性取决于保留哪些特定连接，而非单纯的稀疏度。
3. 在深度维度上，组合性表现出目标依赖性，存在一个峰值范围，过浅或过深均会导致组合性丧失。
4. 当偏离上述条件时，梯度下降倾向于收敛到“破碎的”（fractured）解而非组合性解。

Conclusion: 组合性并非深度学习的默认属性，而是仅在特定的网络结构（深度与稀疏度）下才会显现。通过合理的剪枝策略与深度预测，可以显著提升模型发现组合性解的能力。该研究为理解神经网络的泛化机制提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Compositionality is believed to be the foundation for generalization, enabling models to reuse meaningful primitives in novel combinations. Yet, models trained with standard gradient-based optimization rarely, and often only weakly, exhibit compositional internal structure, and it remains unclear how or why such compositionality forms. In this work, we show that compositionality emerges in a narrow connectivity-depth sweet spot. Along the connectivity axis, compositionality only appears in some specifically sparse networks, heavily depends on which connections remain rather than on weights' sparsity alone. Along the depth axis, compositionality emerges within a narrow, target-dependent regime, peaking at specific depths, while both shallower and deeper networks fail. When either the depth or connectivity condition is violated, gradient descent silently converges to fractured solutions rather than compositional ones. To discover and exploit this emergence, we introduce (i) similarity-based pruning (SP) to recover compositional connectivity and (ii) a heuristic depth predictor to estimate where compositionality is most likely to appear. Finally, we support these empirical findings with a theoretical framework based on compositional sparsity, volume-ratio arguments, and feature-interference bounds, explaining why compositional solutions are reachable only in a narrow depth-connectivity regime.

Beyond quantitative performance, the results highlight that aggregation poses greater complexity and challenges than simplification, underscoring the difficulty of capturing higher-level spatial relationships in map generalization with current deep learning approaches.
